10.01.001/0 śrī-rājovāca
10.01.001/1 kathito vaṃśa-vistāro bhavatā soma-sūryayoḥ
10.01.001/3 rājñāṃ cobhaya-vaṃśyānāṃ caritaṃ paramādbhutam
10.01.002/1 yadoś ca dharma-śīlasya nitarāṃ muni-sattama
10.01.002/3 tatrāṃśenāvatīrṇasya viṣṇor vīryāṇi śaṃsa naḥ
10.01.003/1 avatīrya yador vaṃśe bhagavān bhūta-bhāvanaḥ
10.01.003/3 kṛtavān yāni viśvātmā tāni no vada vistarāt
10.01.004/1 nivṛtta-tarṣair upagīyamānād bhavauṣadhāc chrotra-mano-'bhirāmāt

10.01.006/1 drauṇy-astra-vipluṣṭam idaṃ mad-aṅgaṃ santāna-bījaṃ kuru-pāṇḍavānām

10.01.008/3 devakyā garbha-sambandhaḥ kuto dehāntaraṃ vinā

10.01.010/1 vraje vasan kim akaron madhupuryāṃ ca keśavaḥ

10.01.011/3 yadu-puryāṃ sahāvātsīt patnyaḥ katy abhavan prabhoḥ

10.01.012/3 vaktum arhasi sarvajña śraddadhānāya vistṛtam

10.01.013/3 pibantaṃ tvan-mukhāmbhoja- cyutaṃ hari-kathāmṛtam

10.01.014/1 evaṃ niśamya bhṛgu-nandana sādhu-vādaṃ

10.01.014/4 vyāhartum ārabhata bhāgavata-pradhānaḥ
10.01.015/0 śrī-śuka uvāca
10.01.015/1 samyag vyavasitā buddhis tava rājarṣi-sattama

10.01.016/1 vāsudeva-kathā-praśnaḥ puruṣāṃs trīn punāti hi
10.01.016/3 vaktāraṃ pracchakaṃ śrotṝṃs tat-pāda-salilaṃ yathā

10.01.021/1 giraṃ samādhau gagane samīritāṃ niśamya vedhās tridaśān uvāca ha
10.01.021/3 gāṃ pauruṣīṃ me śṛṇutāmarāḥ punar vidhīyatām āśu tathaiva mā ciram
10.01.022/1 puraiva puṃsāvadhṛto dharā-jvaro bhavadbhir aṃśair yaduṣūpajanyatām
10.01.022/3 sa yāvad urvyā bharam īśvareśvaraḥ sva-kāla-śaktyā kṣapayaṃś cared bhuvi

10.01.023/3 janiṣyate tat-priyārthaṃ sambhavantu sura-striyaḥ

10.01.027/3 māthurāñ chūrasenāṃś ca viṣayān bubhuje purā

10.01.030/1 ugrasena-sutaḥ kaṃsaḥ svasuḥ priya-cikīrṣayā
10.01.030/3 raśmīn hayānāṃ jagrāha raukmai ratha-śatair vṛtaḥ
10.01.031/1 catuḥ-śataṃ pāribarhaṃ gajānāṃ hema-mālinām

10.01.032/3 duhitre devakaḥ prādād yāne duhitṛ-vatsalaḥ
10.01.033/1 śaṅkha-tūrya-mṛdaṅgāś ca nedur dundubhayaḥ samam

10.01.034/3 asyās tvām aṣṭamo garbho hantā yāṃ vahase 'budha

10.01.035/3 bhaginīṃ hantum ārabdhaṃ khaḍga-pāṇiḥ kace 'grahīt

10.01.036/3 vasudevo mahā-bhāga uvāca parisāntvayan
10.01.037/0 śrī-vasudeva uvāca
10.01.037/1 ślāghanīya-guṇaḥ śūrair bhavān bhoja-yaśaskaraḥ
10.01.037/3 sa kathaṃ bhaginīṃ hanyāt striyam udvāha-parvaṇi
10.01.038/1 mṛtyur janmavatāṃ vīra dehena saha jāyate
10.01.038/3 adya vābda-śatānte vā mṛtyur vai prāṇināṃ dhruvaḥ
10.01.039/1 dehe pañcatvam āpanne dehī karmānugo 'vaśaḥ
10.01.039/3 dehāntaram anuprāpya prāktanaṃ tyajate vapuḥ
10.01.040/1 vrajaṃs tiṣṭhan padaikena yathaivaikena gacchati
10.01.040/3 yathā tṛṇa-jalaukaivaṃ dehī karma-gatiṃ gataḥ
10.01.041/1 svapne yathā paśyati deham īdṛśaṃ manorathenābhiniviṣṭa-cetanaḥ

10.01.043/2 samīra-vegānugataṃ vibhāvyate

10.01.046/0 śrī-śuka uvāca
10.01.046/1 evaṃ sa sāmabhir bhedair bodhyamāno 'pi dāruṇaḥ
10.01.046/3 na nyavartata kauravya puruṣādān anuvrataḥ

10.01.055/0 śrī-śuka uvāca

10.01.064/3 bhūmer bhārāyamāṇānāṃ daityānāṃ ca vadhodyamam
10.01.065/1 ṛṣer vinirgame kaṃso yadūn matvā surān iti
